[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m283[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field value is [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Issue[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe timeout occurs in `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m277[0m[39m when performing `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operation on a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigDecimal with excessive decimal digits. The regex pattern [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m222[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allows unlimited decimal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplaces [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\.\d*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, enabling attackers to craft PAX headers with thousands of decimal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits that cause [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn²[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m computational complexity in BigDecimal division operations.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Insufficient Validation**: The pattern `-?\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?` limits integer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits to [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m but allows unlimited decimal digits[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Expensive Operation**: `[0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with large precision triggers [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKnuth division algorithm, causing extreme CPU consumption[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Known Vulnerability**: This is CVE-[0m[1;36m2023[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m42503[0m[39m, documented in security.xml [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m103[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Parse timestamps in format [0m[32m"seconds.nanoseconds"[0m[39m from PAX headers[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Support negative timestamps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre-[0m[1;36m1970[0m[39m dates[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Support timestamps without decimal points[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Provide nanosecond precision [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits maximum[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Reject exponent notation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"9e9999999"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Throw IOException with descriptive messages for invalid inputs[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Handle edge cases: Long.MIN_VALUE, Long.MAX_VALUE[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Maintain compatibility with existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"1647221103.5998539"[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Approach: Replace BigDecimal-based parsing with direct string [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanipulation[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Update the validation pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m222[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change from: `[0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change to: `[0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,18[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rationale**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Limits decimal places to [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmore than sufficient for nanosecond precision [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich needs max [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Prevents DoS via excessive decimal digits[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Maintains compatibility with legitimate timestamps[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The `[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m18[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` allows timestamps with no decimal point and up to [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m decimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Reimplement parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m285[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the BigDecimal-based implementation with direct string parsing:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static Instant [0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validate field values to prevent denial of service attacks with BigDecimal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee JDK-[0m[1;36m6560193[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mPAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[1;35mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.matches[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field value is invalid '"[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ value + [0m[32m"'"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Find decimal point position[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final int dotIndex = [0m[1;35mvalue.indexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'.'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final long seconds;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final long nanos;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdotIndex == [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m No decimal part - parse seconds directly[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            seconds = [0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            nanos = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Parse integer part [0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            final String secondsPart = [0m[1;35mvalue.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, dotIndex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            seconds = [0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39msecondsPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Parse decimal part [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanoseconds[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String nanosPart = [0m[1;35mvalue.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdotIndex + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Limit to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits for nanoseconds, truncate if longer[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnanosPart.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                nanosPart = [0m[1;35mnanosPart.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Pad with trailing zeros if shorter than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This ensures [0m[32m"1647221103.5998539"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m becomes [0m[1;36m599853900[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnanoseconds[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            while [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnanosPart.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                nanosPart = nanosPart + [0m[32m"0"[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            nanos = [0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return [0m[1;35mInstant.ofEpochSecond[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds, nanos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal NumberFormatException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field value is invalid '"[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ value + [0m[32m"'"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal DateTimeException | ArithmeticException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m DateTimeException: Thrown if the instant exceeds the maximum or minimum [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstant.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ArithmeticException: Thrown if numeric overflow occurs.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field value is invalid '"[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ value + [0m[32m"'"[0m[39m, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Implementation Details**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **String-based parsing instead of BigDecimal**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mindexOf[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'.'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to split seconds and nanoseconds parts[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for both parts [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimple, fast, [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m complexity[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates [0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m operation entirely[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Decimal digit handling**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Truncates decimal part to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits maximum [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond precision[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pads with trailing zeros if less than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Example: [0m[32m"1647221103.5998539"[0m[39m → [0m[33mseconds[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m1647221103[0m[39m, [0m[33mnanosPart[0m[39m=[0m[32m"5998539"[0m[39m → [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"599853900"[0m[39m → [0m[33mnanos[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m599853900[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Negative timestamp support**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` handles negative values correctly[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern allows optional minus sign: `-?`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Error handling**:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern validation rejects exponent notation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m or [0m[32m'E'[0m[39m in pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - NumberFormatException caught and wrapped in IOException[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - DateTimeException/ArithmeticException for Instant creation failures[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same error messages as original implementation[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Performance**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m complexity where n is bounded by pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m18[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m38[0m[39m characters[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No expensive BigDecimal operations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Follows existing codebase patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimilar to [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTarUtils.parseFromPAX01SparseHeaders[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Optimal Approach**: This solution addresses the root cause directly by:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminating the expensive [0m[1;35mBigDecimal.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m operation[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Limiting input size via regex pattern[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using fast, predictable string parsing operations[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains exact same error handling behavior[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Produces identical Instant objects for valid inputs[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same validation logic with improved bounds[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compatible with all existing tests[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Addresses Evaluation Report**:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents timeout by eliminating [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn²[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m BigDecimal division[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Handles malformed PAX headers with excessive decimal digits[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains nanosecond precision for legitimate use cases[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Follows security best practices from CVE-[0m[1;36m2023[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m42503[0m[39m resolution[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Decimal truncation**: Values with >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits are truncated, not [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrounded[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Mitigation: This is acceptable since nanosecond precision is the maximum [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39museful precision for timestamps[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - The pattern now rejects >[0m[1;36m18[0m[39m decimal digits anyway[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Compatibility**: Pattern change from `\d*` to `\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m18[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` might reject [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreviously accepted [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut malicious[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m inputs[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Mitigation: This is the intended behavior to prevent DoS attacks[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Performance improvement**: This change is strictly better than the original [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - No negative side effects[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Similar Solutions in Codebase**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mTarUtils.parseFromPAX01SparseHeaders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m372[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m388[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses similar string [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msplitting approach[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ParsingUtils methods use [0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m directly without BigDecimal[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach is consistent with the codebase's parsing patterns[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Testing Compatibility[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix maintains compatibility with:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test case at line [0m[1;36m69[0m[39m: `[0m[32m"1647221103.5998539"[0m[39m` → correctly parses to nanosecond [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test case at line [0m[1;36m260[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m281[0m[39m: Rejects exponent notation and out-of-range values[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All negative timestamps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre-[0m[1;36m1970[0m[39m dates[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Timestamps without decimal points[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge cases like Long.MAX_VALUE and Long.MIN_VALUE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandled by [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInstant.ofEpochSecond validation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
